SELECT first.plate, other.plate,   COUNT(DISTINCT other.mjd) + COUNT(DISTINCT first.mjd) AS nightsObserved,   otherPlate.programname, count(DISTINCT other.bestObjID) AS objects  FROM SpecObjAll first  JOIN SpecObjAll other ON first.bestObjID = other.bestObjID  JOIN PlateX AS firstPlate ON firstPlate.plate = first.plate  JOIN PlateX AS otherPlate ON otherPlate.plate = other.plate  WHERE first.scienceprimary = # AND other.scienceprimary = #   AND other.bestObjID > #  GROUP BY first.plate, other.plate, otherPlate.programname  ORDER BY nightsObserved DESC, otherPlate.programname,   first.plate, other.plate

SELECT TOP #   SPhot.specObjID,    -- DR8+ spectroscopic ID   SPhot.objID,        -- DR8+ photometric ID   S7.dr7ObjID,        -- DR7- photometric ID      SObj.mjd,           -- Modified Julian Date of observation   SObj.plate,         -- plate ID   SObj.fiberID,       -- Fiber ID      SObj.z,             -- (spectroscopic) redshift    SObj.zErr,          -- redshift error      SObj.ra,            -- fiber Right Ascencion   SObj.dec,          -- fiber Declination      SObj.snMedian_u,    -- Median S/N in u-band   SObj.snMedian_g,    -- Median S/N in g-band   SObj.snMedian_r,    -- Median S/N in r-band   SObj.snMedian_i,    -- Median S/N in i-band   SObj.snMedian_z,    -- Median S/N in z-band        gSL.h_alpha_eqw,    -- H_alpha equivalent width    gSL.h_alpha_eqw_err -- H_alpha equivalent wdith error             FROM dr1#.SpecPhoto AS SPhot   JOIN dr1#.SpecObj AS SObj ON SObj.specObjID = SPhot.specObjID   JOIN dr1#.galSpecLine AS gSL ON gSL.specObjID = SPhot.specObjID   JOIN dr1#.SpecDR7 AS S7 ON S7.specObjID = SPhot.specObjID   JOIN dr1#.emissionLinesPort AS ELP ON ELP.specObjID = SPhot.specObjID      --dr1#.galSpecLine AS gSL,   --dr1#.SpecLineNames AS LN1   --dr7.SpecObj as SObj    WHERE SObj.zWarning = #   AND gSL.h_alpha_eqw > #   AND ELP.bpt = Star Forming
SELECT TOP #   SPhot.specObjID,    -- DR8+ spectroscopic ID   SPhot.objID,        -- DR8+ photometric ID   S7.dr7ObjID,        -- DR7- photometric ID      SObj.mjd,           -- Modified Julian Date of observation   SObj.plate,         -- plate ID   SObj.fiberID,       -- Fiber ID      SObj.z,             -- (spectroscopic) redshift    SObj.zErr,          -- redshift error      SObj.ra,            -- fiber Right Ascencion   SObj.dec,          -- fiber Declination      SObj.snMedian_u,    -- Median S/N in u-band   SObj.snMedian_g,    -- Median S/N in g-band   SObj.snMedian_r,    -- Median S/N in r-band   SObj.snMedian_i,    -- Median S/N in i-band   SObj.snMedian_z,    -- Median S/N in z-band        gSL.h_alpha_eqw,    -- H_alpha equivalent width    gSL.h_alpha_eqw_err -- H_alpha equivalent wdith error             FROM dr1#.SpecPhoto AS SPhot   JOIN dr1#.SpecObj AS SObj ON SObj.specObjID = SPhot.specObjID   JOIN dr1#.galSpecLine AS gSL ON gSL.specObjID = SPhot.specObjID   JOIN dr1#.SpecDR7 AS S7 ON S7.specObjID = SPhot.specObjID   JOIN dr1#.emissionLinesPort AS ELP ON ELP.specObjID = SPhot.specObjID      --dr1#.galSpecLine AS gSL,   --dr1#.SpecLineNames AS LN1   --dr7.SpecObj as SObj    WHERE SObj.zWarning = #   AND gSL.h_alpha_eqw > #   AND ELP.BPT = Star Forming

SELECT TOP # p.objid, p.ra,p.dec,p.petror9#_r, p.dered_g, p.dered_r, s.z as z_spec, s.zErr, zns.nvote, zns.p_el as elliptical, zns.p_cw as spiralclock, zns.p_acw as spiralanticlock, zns.p_edge as edgeon, zns.p_dk as dontknow, zns.p_mg as merger   FROM Galaxy as p    JOIN ZooNoSpec AS zns ON p.objid = zns.objid    JOIN SpecObj AS s ON s.bestobjid = p.objid WHERE s.z BETWEEN # AND #
SELECT TOP # p.objid, p.ra,p.dec,p.petror9#_r, p.dered_r, p.dered_g, s.bestobjid, s.z, s.zErr, zms.p_el_mon, zms.nvote_mon   FROM Galaxy as p    JOIN zooMonochromeBias AS zms ON p.objid = zms.objid    JOIN SpecObj AS s ON s.bestobjid = p.objid WHERE p.clean=# and zms.nvote_mon >= # and  zms.p_el_mon> .# and s.z > .# and s.z < .#
select  top # OS.objID,OS.clean, OS.u, OS.g, OS.r, OS.i ,OS.z,  OS.u_err, OS.g_err, OS.r_err, OS.i_err, OS.z_err, OS.ra, OS.dec, OS.ra_err, OS.dec_err, OS.RowNumber into mydb.filtered_full from ( 	select 	objID, clean, 	psfMag_u - extinction_u as u, 	psfMag_g - extinction_g as g, 	psfMag_r - extinction_R as r, 	psfMag_i - extinction_i as i, 	psfMag_z - extinction_z as z, 	psfMagErr_u as u_err, 	psfMagErr_g as g_err, 	psfMagErr_r as r_err, 	psfMagErr_i as i_err, 	psfMagErr_z as z_err, 	ra, dec, raErr as ra_err, decErr as dec_err, 	ROW_NUMBER() over (order by dec) as RowNumber 	 	from star 	 	where 	CLEAN = # AND 	ra BETWEEN # and # AND 	dec BETWEEN # and # AND 	psfMag_r < # AND         psfMag_g < # AND         psfMag_g - psfMag_r < #   	 ) as OS  where OS.RowNumber % # = #
